country_event = { #武德励进会宣告成立
	id = NKRsichuan.1
	title = NKRsichuan.1.t
	desc = NKRsichuan.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_liu_xiang_suit

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuan.1 option NKRsichuan.1.a"
		name = NKRsichuan.1.a
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			name = SZC_WDLJH_party
			long_name = SZC_WDLJH_party_long
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = NKRsichuan.2
				days = 3
			}
			country_event = {
				id = NKRsichuan.3
				days = 6
			}
			country_event = {
				id = NKRsichuan.4
				days = 9
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #刘湘之死
	id = NKRsichuan.13
	title = NKRsichuan.13.t
	desc = NKRsichuan.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_liu_xiang_suit

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuan.13 option NKRsichuan.13.a"
		name = NKRsichuan.13.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = SZC_liu_xiang_dead_tooltip
		effect_tooltip = {
			SZC_liu_xiang = {
				kill_character = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SZC_liu_xiang = {
				retire_character = yes
				retire = yes
			}
			SZC_power_vacuum = {
				promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			set_country_flag = SZC_liu_xiang_dead
			add_ideas = { SZC_after_liu }
		}
		country_lock_all_division_template = yes
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #惨剧定性
	id = NKRsichuan.28
	title = NKRsichuan.28.t
	desc = NKRsichuan.28.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_dongdalu

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {#有罪！
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuan.28 option NKRsichuan.28.a"
		name = NKRsichuan.28.a
		SZC_liu_congyun = {
			kill_character = yes
		}
		add_ideas = {
			SZC_yiguandao_revolt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = NKRsichuan_YCPpath
			}
			country_event = {
				id = NKRsichuan.30
				days = 3
			}
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = NKRsichuan.29
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #潘文华巩固政权
	id = NKRsichuan.29
	title = NKRsichuan.29.t
	desc = NKRsichuan.29.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_pan_wenhua_2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {#总有人得收拾残局。
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuan.29 option NKRsichuan.29.a"
		name = NKRsichuan.29.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = focus_tree_will_change_tt
		set_country_flag = NKRSZCpanpath
		activate_advisor = SZC_li_hongkun_sic
		load_focus_tree = Sichuan_Clique_Panwenhua
		complete_national_focus = SZC_Pan_Victory
		SZC_pan_wenhua = {
			promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			promote_leader = yes
			promote_to_field_marshal = yes
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SZC_after_liu
			add_idea = SZC_after_liu_2
		}
		add_ideas = {
			SZC_pan_legitimacy_1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = SZC_WDLJH_PWH_party_long
				name = SZC_WDLJH_PWH_party
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #中国青年党浮出水面
	id = NKRsichuan.31
	title = NKRsichuan.31.t
	desc = NKRsichuan.31.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_YCP

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {#青年中国，自川蜀而始！
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuan.31 option NKRsichuan.31.a"
		name = NKRsichuan.31.a
		SZC_li_huang = {
			promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_statist_subtype
		}
		SZC_zeng_qi = {
			promote_character = paternal_autocrat_statist_subtype
		}
		SZC_zhang_bolun = {
			promote_character = market_liberal_subtype
		}
		SZC_xia_taosheng = {
			SZC_recruit_character_effect = yes
			promote_character = social_conservative_statist_subtype
		}
		SZC_jiang_yungang = {
			SZC_recruit_character_effect = yes
			promote_character = national_populist_strum_drang_statist_subtype
		}
		SZC_zuo_shunsheng = {
			SZC_recruit_character_effect = yes
			promote_character = social_liberal_constitutional_statist_subtype
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SZC_politic_changes_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = SZC_YCP_xingshe_party_long
				name = SZC_YCP_xingshe_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = SZC_YCP_shenshe_party_long
				name = SZC_YCP_shenshe_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = SZC_NSP_party_long
				name = SZC_NSP_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name = SZC_YCP_zhongshe_party_long
				name = SZC_YCP_zhongshe_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				long_name = SZC_YCP_tishe_party_long
				name = SZC_YCP_tishe_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				long_name = SZC_YCP_zhaoxishe_party_long
				name = SZC_YCP_zhaoxishe_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_populist
				long_name = SZC_YCP_guohunshe_party_long
				name = SZC_YCP_guohunshe_party
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 0.15
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 0.15
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = national_populist
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			SZC_tang_shizun = {
				set_portraits = {
					army = {
						large = GFX_portrait_SZC_tang_shizun_YCP_large
						small = GFX_portrait_SZC_tang_shizun_YCP_small
					}
				}
			}
			SZC_fan_shaozeng = {
				set_portraits = {
					army = {
						large = GFX_portrait_SZC_fan_shaozeng_ycp_large
						small = GFX_portrait_SZC_fan_shaozeng_ycp_small
					}
				}
			}
			SZC_wang_lingji = {
				set_portraits = {
					army = {
						large = GFX_portrait_SZC_wang_lingji_ycp_large
						small = GFX_portrait_SZC_wang_lingji_ycp_small
					}
				}

		}

country_event = { #革命志士
	id = NKRsichuan.171
	title = NKRsichuan.171.t
	desc = NKRsichuan.171.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_pan_wenhua

	is_triggered_only = yes
	

	option = {#
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuan.171 option NKRsichuan.171.a"
		name = NKRsichuan.171.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SZC_pan_wenhua = {
				promote_character = radical_socialist_revolutionary_tridemist_subtype
			}
			end_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:paternal_autocrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = {
					has_socialist_government = no
					NOT = {
						original_tag = JAP
						original_tag = KOR
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = radical_socialist
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_subject = JAP }
				JAP_socialist_government = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_subject = KOR }
				KOR = {
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
					KOR_socialist_government = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_subject = INC }
				INC = {
					INC_puppet_setup = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes
	

	option = {#谁能允许我们禁锢工人的自由？

		name = NKRsichuan.490.a
		add_political_power = 25
	}
	option = {#只有将其置于国有才能保证不受到社会主义侵蚀。

		name = NKRsichuan.490.b
		add_political_power = -50
		add_ideas = {
			SZC_YCP_state_union_idea
		}
	}
	option = {#与张国焘的合作值得一试。

		name = NKRsichuan.490.c
		add_political_power = -10
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = NKRsichuan.491
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #妇女权利？
	id = NKRsichuan.497
	title = NKRsichuan.497.t
	desc = NKRsichuan.497.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_dongdalu

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	

	option = {#妇女无权则平等无望！
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuan.497 option NKRsichuan.497.a"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						var = YCP_adv_chk
						value = token:SZC_yu_xiaoquan
					}
					SZC_yu_xiaoquan = {
						YCP_working_in_party = yes
					}
				}
				AND = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						var = YCP_adv_chk
						value = token:SZC_tan_tiwu
					}
					SZC_tan_tiwu = {
						YCP_working_in_party = yes
					}
				}
				OR = {
					SZC_yu_xiaoquan = { is_hired_as_advisor = yes}
					SZC_tan_tiwu = { is_hired_as_advisor = yes}
				}
			}
		}
		name = NKRsichuan.497.a
		add_stability = -0.1
		SZC_YCP_constitution_progress_effect = yes
		set_country_flag = SZC_YCP_female_rights_guaranteed
	}
	option = {#我们将循序渐进，而非执着于空谈乱想。
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuan.497 option NKRsichuan.497.b"
		name = NKRsichuan.497.b
		SZC_YCP_constitution_conservative_effect = yes
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
}

	desc = NKRsichuan.519.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	

	option = {#怎么样呢？
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuan.519 option NKRsichuan.519.a"
		name = NKRsichuan.519.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SZC_YCP_progress_constitution
				}
				country_event = {
					id = NKRsichuan.522
					days = 3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SZC_YCP_moderate_constitution
				}
				country_event = {
					id = NKRsichuan.521
					days = 3
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = NKRsichuan.520
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #保守革命的遗产
	id = NKRsichuan.677
	title = NKRsichuan.677.t
	desc = NKRsichuan.677.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_dongdalu

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			annexations_reset_german_tags = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_german_unifier_tag = yes
						AND = {
							64 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Brandenburg
							owns_state = 147 #Prussian Saxony
						}
						AND = {
							AUS_can_form_germany = yes
							OR = {
								has_subject = BAY
								any_owned_state = {
									is_south_germany = yes
									state_strategic_value > 89
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			annexations_create_german_event_targets = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					annexations_germany_is_independent_ally_or_puppet_of_ROOT = no
					PRE = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
				}
				PRE = { save_event_target_as = prussia add_to_array = { ROOT.potential_grant_targets = THIS } }
			}
			58 = { retain_state = yes } #Schleswig-Holstein
		}
	}

	option = {#骑士精神再现。
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuan.677 option NKRsichuan.677.a"
		name = NKRsichuan.677.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = NKRsichuan.677.tt
		annexations_release_republican_germany = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			GRU_edgar_jung = {
				set_nationality = GRU
			}
			GRU = {
				GRU_edgar_jung = {
					promote_character = national_populist_strum_drang_statist_subtype
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = GRU_HRR
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = national_populist
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = national_populist
					name = GRU_BDR_party
					long_name = GRU_BDR_party_long
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = national_populist
					popularity = 0.4
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
			}
		}
		activate_advisor = QIE_hu_shih_sic
		set_country_leader_ideology = market_liberal_clientelist_subtype

				remove_idea = SZC_YCP_progress_constitution
				add_idea = SZC_YCP_presidental_constitution_idea
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SZC_YCP_conservative_constitution
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_YCP_conservative_constitution
				add_idea = SZC_YCP_presidental_constitution_idea
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SZC_YCP_moderate_constitution
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_YCP_moderate_constitution
				add_idea = SZC_YCP_presidental_constitution_idea
			}
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			name = SZC_PYCP_CDP_1_party
			long_name = SZC_PYCP_CDP_1_party_long
		}

country_event = { #政变
	id = NKRsichuan.731
	title = NKRsichuan.731.t
	desc = NKRsichuan.731.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_dongdalu

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	

	option = {#尘埃落定。
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuan.731 option NKRsichuan.731.a"
		name = NKRsichuan.731.a
		SZC_zhang_guotao = {
			kill_character = yes
		}
		SZC_chen_zaidao = {
			promote_character = paternal_autocrat_stratocracy_subtype
			add_trait = {
				trait = SZC_YCP_supreme_marshall
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_stratocracy_subtype
			}
			add_trait = {
				trait = SZC_YCP_the_lion
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_stratocracy_subtype
			}
			set_portraits = {
				army = {
					large = GFX_portrait_SZC_chen_zaidao_marshall_large
					small = GFX_portrait_SZC_chen_zaidao_marshall_small
				}
			}
		}
		
		activate_advisor = SZC_xu_shiyou_sic
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
		}
		uncomplete_national_focus = {
			focus = SZC_YCP_use_civilian_parties
			uncomplete_children = no
			refund_political_power = no
		}
		uncomplete_national_focus = {
			focus = SZC_YCP_YCPs_legacy
			uncomplete_children = no
			refund_political_power = no
		}
		uncomplete_national_focus = {
			focus = SZC_YCP_restore_parliament_as_rubber_stamp
			uncomplete_children = no
			refund_political_power = no
		}
		uncomplete_national_focus = {
			focus = SZC_YCP_presidents_advisors
			uncomplete_children = no
			refund_political_power = no
		}
		unlock_national_focus = SZC_YCP_expand_army_allowances
		unlock_national_focus = SZC_YCP_generals_know_best
		unlock_national_focus = SZC_YCP_new_age_of_peoples_democracy
		unlock_national_focus = SZC_YCP_national_guard
		
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SZC_YCP_state_socialist_front_3_idea
			add_idea = SZC_YCP_an_army_with_state_3_idea
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 0.35
			}
			remove_idea = SZC_YCP_an_army_with_state_idea
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = {
					has_socialist_government = yes
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = NKRsichuan.732
				days = 3650
			}
			SZC_assorted_leaders_unique = {
				SZC_recruit_character_effect = yes
				promote_character = syndicalist_yellow_syndicalist_subtype
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #516革命-工团
	id = NKRsichuanpuppet.1
	title = NKRsichuanpuppet.1.t
	desc = NKRsichuanpuppet.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_516

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			SZC_park_chunghee = {
				SZC_recruit_character_effect = yes
				set_nationality = KOR
			}
			KOR = {
				SZC_park_chunghee = {
					promote_character = syndicalist_peoples_democracy_subtype
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = syndicalist
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = syndicalist
					name = KOR_park_party
					long_name = KOR_park_name_long
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = syndicalist
					popularity = 0.3
				}
			}
		}
	}
	

	option = {#我们承认他的革命
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuanpuppet.1 option NKRsichuanpuppet.1.a"
		name = NKRsichuanpuppet.1.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
	}
	option = {#什么？立刻出兵汉城！
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuanpuppet.1 option NKRsichuanpuppet.1.b"
		name = NKRsichuanpuppet.1.b
		set_autonomy = {
			target = KOR
			autonomy_state = autonomy_free
		}
		KOR = {
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = KOR
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #判断
	id = NKRsichuanpuppet.8
	title = NKRsichuanpuppet.8.t
	desc = NKRsichuanpuppet.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_516

	trigger = {
		KOR = {
			is_subject_of = SZC
		}
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = NKRsichuan_YCPpath
			has_country_flag = NKRSZC_CDLpath
			has_country_flag = NKRSZC_joinkmt
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

	hidden = yes
	

	option = {#
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuanpuppet.8 option NKRsichuanpuppet.8.a"
		name = NKRsichuanpuppet.8.a
		country_event = {
			id = NKRsichuanpuppet.9
			days = 365
		}
	}
}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuanpuppet.9 option NKRsichuanpuppet.9.a"
		name = NKRsichuanpuppet.9.a
		news_event = NKRnews.40
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = SZC_qi_nanxun
						}
						has_completed_focus = SZC_pan_socialist_solidarity
					}
					has_country_leader = {
						character = SZC_liu_bocheng
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = NKRsichuanpuppet.1
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = SZC_qi_nanxun
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = SZC_pan_wenhua
						}
						has_socialist_government = yes
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = NKRsichuanpuppet.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = SZC_pan_wenhua
						}
						has_socialist_government = no
					}
					has_country_flag = NKRSZC_CDLpath
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = NKRsichuanpuppet.3
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = SZC_xie_chi
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = NKRsichuanpuppet.5
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = NKRsichuan_YCPpath
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = SZC_YCP_jiang_path
							has_country_flag = SZC_YCP_zeng_hardline_path
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = NKRsichuanpuppet.4
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = SZC_YCP_jiang_path
			}
			country_event = {
				id = NKRsichuanpuppet.6
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = SZC_YCP_zeng_hardline_path
			}
			country_event = {
				id = NKRsichuanpuppet.7
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = NKRsichuanpuppet.30.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			annexations_reset_german_tags = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_german_unifier_tag = yes
						AND = {
							64 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Brandenburg
							owns_state = 147 #Prussian Saxony
						}
						AND = {
							AUS_can_form_germany = yes
							OR = {
								has_subject = BAY
								any_owned_state = {
									is_south_germany = yes
									state_strategic_value > 89
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			annexations_create_german_event_targets = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					annexations_germany_is_independent_ally_or_puppet_of_ROOT = no
					PRE = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
				}
				PRE = { save_event_target_as = prussia add_to_array = { ROOT.potential_grant_targets = THIS } }
			}
			58 = { retain_state = yes } #Schleswig-Holstein
		}
	}

	option = {#
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuanpuppet.30 option NKRsichuanpuppet.30.a"
		name = NKRsichuanpuppet.30.a
		annexations_release_republican_germany = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			GRU_dolf_sternberger = {
				set_nationality = GRU
			}
			GRU = {
				GRU_dolf_sternberger = {
					promote_character = social_democrat_new_legalist_state_socialist_subtype
				}
				GRU_dolf_sternberger = {
					promote_character = social_liberal_constitutional_statist_subtype
				}
				GRU_dolf_sternberger = {
					promote_character = social_conservative_statist_subtype
				}
				GRU_dolf_sternberger = {
					promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_statist_subtype
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = GRU_YCP
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_democrat
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					name = GRU_YCP_party
					long_name = GRU_YCP_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_liberal
					name = GRU_YCP_party
					long_name = GRU_YCP_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					name = GRU_YCP_party
					long_name = GRU_YCP_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					name = GRU_YCP_party
					long_name = GRU_YCP_party_long
				}
			}
		}

country_event = { #民主党转变
	id = NKRsichuanpuppet.32
	title = NKRsichuanpuppet.32.t
	desc = NKRsichuanpuppet.32.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_YCP

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { country_exists = NEE } }
				NEE = { clear_cores_of_tag_if_possible = yes }
			}
			every_state = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_mainland_america = yes
							is_american_pacific_islands = yes
							state = 463 #Alaska
						}
					}
					add_core_of = USA
				}
				else = {
					remove_core_of = USA
				}
				remove_core_of = WCA
				remove_core_of = ACC
				remove_core_of = APG
				remove_claim_by = USA
				remove_claim_by = WCA
				remove_claim_by = ACC
				remove_claim_by = APG
			}
			463 = { retain_state = yes } #Alaska
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_american_pacific_islands = yes }
				add_core_of = HAW
				retain_state = yes
			}
			WCA = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_character = WCA_jack_reed }
					retire_character = WCA_jack_reed
				}
			}
			USA = {
				USA_swap_to_blue_cosmetic_tag = yes
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_character = USA_douglas_macarthur } }
					USA_douglas_macarthur = { set_nationality = USA }
					promote_character = { character = USA_douglas_macarthur ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					HAW = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						has_country_leader = {
							character = HAW_yau_leongfong
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = NKRsichuanpuppet.48 days = 56 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {#
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuanpuppet.32 option NKRsichuanpuppet.32.a"
		name = NKRsichuanpuppet.32.a
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = USA }
		release_targeted_tag_nocosmetic = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			var:tag_to_release = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = USA_back_in_business }
					uncomplete_national_focus = { focus = USA_back_in_business uncomplete_children = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_hebert_agar = {
				set_nationality = USA
			}
			USA = {
				USA_hebert_agar = {
					promote_character = social_democrat_new_legalist_state_socialist_subtype
				}
				USA_hebert_agar = {
					promote_character = social_liberal_constitutional_statist_subtype
				}
				USA_hebert_agar = {
					promote_character = social_conservative_statist_subtype
				}
				USA_hebert_agar = {
					promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_statist_subtype
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = USA_YCP
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					name = USA_YCP_party
					long_name = USA_YCP_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_liberal
					name = USA_YCP_party
					long_name = USA_YCP_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					name = USA_YCP_party
					long_name = USA_YCP_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					name = USA_YCP_party
					long_name = USA_YCP_party_long
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #青年波兰复兴
	id = NKRsichuanpuppet.33
	title = NKRsichuanpuppet.33.t
	desc = NKRsichuanpuppet.33.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_YCP

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_poland = no }
				remove_claim_by = POL
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { core_countries^num > 1 } }
					remove_core_of = POL
				}
			}
			POL = {
				POL_clear_economy = yes
				POL_remove_monarchy = yes
				POL_remove_guderian = yes
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				remove_ideas = {
					POL_uprising
					POL_uprising2
					POL_uprising3
					POL_ZRP
					POL_OZN_ONR_infighting
					POL_uprising_crash1
					POL_uprising_crash2
					POL_uprising_crash3
					POL_uprising_crash4
					POL_uprising_crash5
					POL_uprising_crash6
					POL_recovering_eco1
					POL_recovering_eco2
					POL_recovering_eco3
					POL_crescendo_of_blood
					POL_suppressing_rival_government
					POL_revolutionary_factionalism
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_character = AUS_karl_albrecht_von_habsburg }
					AUS_karl_albrecht_von_habsburg = {
						set_character_name = AUS_karl_albrecht_von_habsburg
						set_character_as_republican = yes
						remove_all_country_leader_roles = yes
						if = {
							limit = { AUS = { AUS_is_led_by_habsburgs = yes } }
							set_nationality = AUS
						}
						else = {

country_event = { #起源之地-姜人
	id = NKRsichuanpuppet.39
	title = NKRsichuanpuppet.39.t
	desc = NKRsichuanpuppet.39.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_YCP

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { country_exists = FRA } }
				FRA = { clear_cores_of_tag_if_possible = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { country_exists = NFA } }
				NFA = { clear_cores_of_tag_if_possible = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { country_exists = FRP } }
				FRP = {
					clear_cores_of_tag_if_possible = yes
					if = {
						limit = { has_character = GER_fedor_von_bock }
						GER_fedor_von_bock = {
							remove_all_country_leader_roles = yes
							set_nationality = GER
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { country_exists = LIL } }
				LIL = {
					clear_cores_of_tag_if_possible = yes
					if = {
						limit = { has_character = GER_roland_koster }
						GER_roland_koster = {
							remove_all_country_leader_roles = yes
							set_nationality = GER
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_french_tag = yes }
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_french_tag = yes
					is_ally_with = ROOT
					OR = {
						is_subject = no
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = france add_to_array = { ROOT.potential_grant_targets = THIS }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_event_target = france } }
				if = {
					limit = { FRA = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes } }
					FRA = { save_event_target_as = france add_to_array = { ROOT.potential_grant_targets = THIS } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FRP = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes } }
					FRP = { save_event_target_as = france add_to_array = { ROOT.potential_grant_targets = THIS } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NFA = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes } }
					NFA = { save_event_target_as = france_exile add_to_array = { ROOT.potential_grant_targets = THIS } }
				}
			}
			1 = { retain_state = yes } #Corsica
			14 = { retain_state = yes } #Upper Brittany
			17 = { retain_state = yes } #Pas-de-Calais
			28 = { retain_state = yes } #Alsace-Lorraine
			29 = { retain_state = yes } #Dunkirk
			735 = { retain_state = yes } #Savoy
			762 = { retain_state = yes } #Nice
			779 = { retain_state = yes } #Labourd
			817 = { retain_state = yes } #Roussillon
			943 = { retain_state = yes } #Upper Savoy
			980 = { retain_state = yes } #Lille
			983 = { retain_state = yes } #Brittany
		}
	}


	option = {#
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuanpuppet.39 option NKRsichuanpuppet.39.a"
		name = NKRsichuanpuppet.39.a
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = FRP }
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_france = yes }
			add_core_of = var:tag_to_release
			hidden_effect = { remove_claim_by = var:tag_to_release }
		}
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = NFA }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = NFA
				modifier = NFA_occupied_france
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FRA_robert_brasillach = {
				set_nationality = FRP
			}
			FRP = {
				FRA_robert_brasillach = {
					promote_character = national_populist_strum_drang_statist_subtype
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = FRA_YCP_SD
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = national_populist
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = national_populist
					name = FRA_YCP_party
					long_name = FRA_YCP_party_long
				}
			}
		}
	}

					owns_state = 526
				}
				add_state_claim = 526 #If KMT China totally conquers Japan, will occupy Okinawa like the US, will get an event later to decide to either give it back or "give it independence"
				var:526.owner = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.071 days = 500 random_days = 250 } } #The Ryukyu Revival - Flavorwise needs some time to pass first for the event to make sense
			}
			537 = { retain_state = yes } #South Sakhalin
			555 = { retain_state = yes } #Kuril Islands
			577 = { retain_state = yes } #North Sakhalin
		}
	}

	option = {#
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuanpuppet.46 option NKRsichuanpuppet.46.a"
		name = NKRsichuanpuppet.46.a
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = JAP }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		JAP = {
			# All general puppet effects
			hidden_effect = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_state
				load_focus_tree = japan_subject_focus
				JAP_close_all = yes
				JAP_clear_ideas = yes
				if = {
					limit = { has_character = JAP_hirohito }
					JAP_hirohito = {
						promote_character = social_democrat_subtype
						promote_character = social_liberal_subtype
						promote_character = market_liberal_subtype
						promote_character = social_conservative_subtype
						promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
						promote_character = paternal_autocrat_subtype
						promote_character = national_populist_subtype
	
						set_portraits = { civilian = { large = GFX_portrait_JAP_hirohito_civilian_large_suit } }
						add_trait = { trait = JAP_hirohito_defeat_trait ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
						add_trait = { trait = JAP_hirohito_defeat_trait ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype }
						add_trait = { trait = JAP_hirohito_defeat_trait ideology = national_populist_subtype }
						add_trait = { trait = JAP_hirohito_defeat_trait ideology = social_conservative_subtype }
						add_trait = { trait = JAP_hirohito_defeat_trait ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
						add_trait = { trait = JAP_hirohito_defeat_trait ideology = social_liberal_subtype }
						add_trait = { trait = JAP_hirohito_defeat_trait ideology = social_democrat_subtype }
					}
					set_country_leader_description = { desc = JAP_hirohito_defeat_leader_desc ideology = authoritarian_democrat }
					set_country_leader_description = { desc = JAP_hirohito_defeat_leader_desc ideology = paternal_autocrat }
					set_country_leader_description = { desc = JAP_hirohito_defeat_leader_desc ideology = national_populist }
					set_country_leader_description = { desc = JAP_hirohito_defeat_leader_desc ideology = social_conservative }
					set_country_leader_description = { desc = JAP_hirohito_defeat_leader_desc ideology = market_liberal }
					set_country_leader_description = { desc = JAP_hirohito_defeat_leader_desc ideology = social_liberal }
					set_country_leader_description = { desc = JAP_hirohito_defeat_leader_desc ideology = social_democrat }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_defeated_nation } }
					# Reset all relevant Parties in case natpops were previously in power
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = social_democrat
						name = JAP_social_democrat_party
						long_name = JAP_social_democrat_party_long
					}
					set_party_name = {
						name = JAP_market_liberal_party_kd
						ideology = market_liberal
						long_name = JAP_market_liberal_party_long_kd
					}
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = social_conservative
						name = JAP_social_conservative_party_kd
						long_name = JAP_social_conservative_party_long_kd
					}
				}
				# Setup the other parties
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					long_name = JAP_zantei_gunseifu_long
					name = JAP_zantei_gunseifu
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					long_name = JAP_zantei_gunseifu_long
					name = JAP_zantei_gunseifu
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = national_populist
					long_name = JAP_zantei_gunseifu_long
					name = JAP_zantei_gunseifu
				}
			}
			add_ideas = {
				JAP_shattered_people_idea
				JAP_devastated_national_economy_idea
				JAP_disarmed_nation_idea
			}
			set_country_flag = JAP_defeated_nation
			clr_country_flag = JAP_RKMT_puppet_flag
			clr_country_flag = JAP_nonKMT_chinese_puppet_flag
			clr_country_flag = JAP_authoritarian_puppet_flag
			clr_country_flag = JAP_liberal_puppet_flag
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							has_socialist_government = yes
							china_alignment_left_kuomintang = yes
						}
					}
				}
				JAP_socialist_government = yes
			}
			else = {
				# Includes authoritarian governments confusingly
				JAP_democratic_government = yes
			}
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_ROJ
			if = {
				limit = {

						has_country_flag = SZC_YCP_jiang_path
					}
				}

					JAP_ozaki_yukio = {
						set_portraits = {
							civilian = {

							}
						}

								ideology = national_populist_strum_drang_statist_subtype

								desc = JAP_ozaki_yukio_desc_natpop
							}
						}

					}
					activate_advisor = JAP_kijuro_shidehara_sic
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {

						has_country_flag = SZC_YCP_zeng_hardline_path
					}
				}
				JAP = {
					JAP_ozaki_yukio = {
						set_portraits = {
							civilian = {

country_event = { #檀香山
	id = NKRsichuanpuppet.47
	title = NKRsichuanpuppet.47.t
	desc = NKRsichuanpuppet.47.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_YCP

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				remove_claim_by = HAW
				if = {
					limit = { is_american_pacific_islands = yes }
					add_core_of = HAW
				}
				else = {
					remove_core_of = HAW
				}
			}
			HAW = {
				clr_country_flag = HAW_can_join_factions
				HAW_remove_monarchy = yes
			}
			annexations_create_german_east_asia_event_target = yes
			annexations_create_japan_event_target = yes
			638 = { retain_state = yes } #Guam
			726 = { retain_state = yes } #Samoa
		}
	}

	option = {#
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuanpuppet.47 option NKRsichuanpuppet.47.a"
		name = NKRsichuanpuppet.47.a
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HAW }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		var:tag_to_release = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = HAW_monarchy_restoration }
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = HAW_monarchy_restoration
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_socialist_government = yes
					has_completed_focus = HAW_declare_a_republic
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = HAW_declare_a_republic
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_socialist_government = no
					has_completed_focus = HAW_revolution_succeeds
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = HAW_revolution_succeeds
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
			}
			
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			HAW_yau_leongfong = {
				set_nationality = HAW
			}
			HAW = {
				HAW_yau_leongfong = {
					promote_character = market_liberal_subtype
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = market_liberal
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					USA = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = NKRsichuanpuppet.48 days = 56 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #大越民族党
	id = NKRsichuanpuppet.49
	title = NKRsichuanpuppet.49.t
	desc = NKRsichuanpuppet.49.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_YCP

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { country_exists = INC } }
				clr_global_flag = GEA_Indochina_Uprising_Fired
				INC = {
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
					clear_cores_of_tag_if_possible = yes
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_vietnam = no }
					remove_core_of = VIN
				}
				else = {
					add_core_of = VIN
				}
				remove_claim_by = VIN
			}
			VIN = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = GEA
						annexations_france_can_annex_overseas = yes
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = can_annex
			}
			annexations_create_france_event_target = yes
			annexations_create_german_east_asia_event_target = yes
		}
	}

	option = {#
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuanpuppet.49 option NKRsichuanpuppet.49.a"
		name = NKRsichuanpuppet.49.a
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = VIN }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		INC = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = yes
					has_socialist_government = yes
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = INC_Unification }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_subject = yes }
					overlord = { country_event = { id = indochina_events.1955 hours = 8 } }
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { id = indochina_events.1955 hours = 8 }
				}
			}
		}
		var:tag_to_release = { VIN_puppet_setup = yes }
		hidden_effect = {
			VIN_nguyen_tuongtam = {
				set_nationality = VIN
			}
			VIN = {
				VIN_nguyen_tuongtam = {
					promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_statist_subtype
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					name = VIN_Dai_Viet_party
					long_name = VIN_Dai_Viet_party_long
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
			}
			FROM = { leave_faction = yes }
			add_to_faction = FROM
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					original_tag = TUR
				}
			}
			SZC = { country_event = { id = CHN.foreignpolicy.048 days = 3 } } #TUR joins us
			add_to_faction = FROM
		}
		else = {
			add_to_faction = FROM
		}
		add_political_power = 20
	}
}
